USERMESSAGE #9
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Template System Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides reactive template selection and management for document rendering.
     5→ * Active template is shared across all components via useState and persisted
     6→ * to localStorage so the selection survives page reloads.
     7→ */
     8→
     9→import { onMounted, computed } from 'vue'
    10→import type { Component } from 'vue'
    11→import CoverLetterModern from '~/templates/modern/CoverLetterModern.vue'
    12→import CoverLetterClassic from '~/templates/classic/CoverLetterClassic.vue'
    13→import CoverLetterMinimal from '~/templates/minimal/CoverLetterMinimal.vue'
    14→import ResignationProfessional from '~/templates/resignation-professional/ResignationProfessional.vue'
    15→import ResignationBrief from '~/templates/resignation-brief/ResignationBrief.vue'
    16→
    17→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_template'
    18→
    19→// Template metadata interface
    20→export interface TemplateMetadata {
    21→  name: string
    22→  displayName: string
    23→  description: string
    24→  /** Document type names this template supports (matches DocumentTypeConfig.name) */
    25→  documentTypes: string[]
    26→}
    27→
    28→// Template registry type
    29→export interface TemplateRegistry {
    30→  [key: string]: {
    31→    component: Component
    32→    metadata: TemplateMetadata
    33→  }
    34→}
    35→
    36→/**
    37→ * Template Registry
    38→ *
    39→ * Maps template names to their Vue components and metadata.
    40→ * All templates use the same ParsedData props interface for consistency.
    41→ */
    42→const templates: TemplateRegistry = {
    43→  modern: {
    44→    component: CoverLetterModern,
    45→    metadata: {
    46→      name: 'modern',
    47→      displayName: 'Modern',
    48→      description: 'Professional cover letter template with modern styling and clean typography',
    49→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    50→    },
    51→  },
    52→  classic: {
    53→    component: CoverLetterClassic,
    54→    metadata: {
    55→      name: 'classic',
    56→      displayName: 'Classic',
    57→      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',
    58→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    59→    },
    60→  },
    61→  minimal: {
    62→    component: CoverLetterMinimal,
    63→    metadata: {
    64→      name: 'minimal',
    65→      displayName: 'Minimal',
    66→      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',
    67→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    68→    },
    69→  },
    70→  'resignation-professional': {
    71→    component: ResignationProfessional,
    72→    metadata: {
    73→      name: 'resignation-professional',
    74→      displayName: 'Professional',
    75→      description: 'Formal letterhead layout with sender top-left, date top-right, and clean typography',
    76→      documentTypes: ['resignation-letter'],
    77→    },
    78→  },
    79→  'resignation-brief': {
    80→    component: ResignationBrief,
    81→    metadata: {
    82→      name: 'resignation-brief',
    83→      displayName: 'Brief',
    84→      description: 'Compact, minimal resignation letter with just the essentials',
    85→      documentTypes: ['resignation-letter'],
    86→    },
    87→  },
    88→}
    89→
    90→/**
    91→ * Composable function to use the reactive template system in Vue components.
    92→ *
    93→ * Active template state is shared across all component instances via useState.
    94→ * On mount, the saved localStorage value is restored (client-side only).
    95→ *
    96→ * @returns Reactive template state and control functions
    97→ */
    98→export function useTemplate() {
    99→  // Shared reactive state — useState ensures all components see the same value
   100→  const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => 'modern')
   101→
   102→  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only, runs once per component mount)
   103→  onMounted(() => {
   104→    try {
   105→      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
   106→      if (saved && templates[saved]) {
   107→        activeTemplate.value = saved
   108→      }
   109→    }
   110→    catch {
   111→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
   112→    }
   113→  })
   114→
   115→  /**
   116→   * Switch to a different template and persist the choice to localStorage.
   117→   */
   118→  function setActiveTemplate(name: string) {
   119→    if (!templates[name]) {
   120→      console.warn(`Template "${name}" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`)
   121→      return
   122→    }
   123→    activeTemplate.value = name
   124→    try {
   125→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)
   126→    }
   127→    catch {
   128→      // Ignore storage errors
   129→    }
   130→  }
   131→
   132→  /** Reactive component for the currently active template */
   133→  const currentTemplate = computed<Component | undefined>(
   134→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.component,
   135→  )
   136→
   137→  /** Metadata for the currently active template */
   138→  const currentTemplateMetadata = computed<TemplateMetadata | undefined>(
   139→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.metadata,
   140→  )
   141→
   142→  /** Names of all registered templates */
   143→  function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   144→    return Object.keys(templates)
   145→  }
   146→
   147→  /** Metadata objects for all registered templates */
   148→  function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   149→    return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   150→  }
   151→
   152→  /** Metadata objects for templates that support the given document type */
   153→  function getTemplatesForDocumentType(docType: string): TemplateMetadata[] {
   154→    return Object.values(templates)
   155→      .filter(t => t.metadata.documentTypes.includes(docType))
   156→      .map(t => t.metadata)
   157→  }
   158→
   159→  return {
   160→    activeTemplate,
   161→    setActiveTemplate,
   162→    currentTemplate,
   163→    currentTemplateMetadata,
   164→    getAvailableTemplates,
   165→    getAllTemplateMetadata,
   166→    getTemplatesForDocumentType,
   167→  }
   168→}
   169→

     1→/**
     2→ * XML Parser Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides XML parsing functionality using browser's native DOMParser API.
     5→ * Zero dependencies approach for fast, simple XML parsing (DECISIONS.md Decision 6).
     6→ */
     7→
     8→// TypeScript interfaces matching the XML schema from docs/sample/cover-letter.xml
     9→
    10→export interface Address {
    11→  street: string
    12→  city: string
    13→  state: string
    14→  zipCode: string
    15→}

    19→  email: string

    29→  text: string
    30→}

    33→  employer: string
    34→  achievements: Achievement[]
    35→}

    38→  salutation: string
    39→  introduction: string

    43→  signature: string

    49→  address: Address

    52→export interface ParsedData {
    53→  formatStyle?: string
    54→  applicant: Applicant
    55→  date: string
    56→  recipient: Recipient
    57→  letter: Letter
    58→}
    59→
    60→export interface ValidationResult {
    61→  isValid: boolean
    62→  error?: string
    63→}
    64→
    65→export interface ParseResult {
    66→  success: boolean
    67→  data?: unknown
    68→  error?: string
    69→}
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Helper function to safely extract text content from an XML element
    73→ */
    74→function getTextContent(element: Element | null, tagName: string, parentName: string = 'document'): string {
    75→  if (!element) {
    76→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    77→  }
    78→  const node = element.querySelector(tagName)
    79→  if (!node) {
    80→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    81→  }
    82→  return node.textContent?.trim() || ''
    83→}
    84→
    85→/**
    86→ * Parse address element (reusable for applicant and recipient addresses)
    87→ */
    88→function parseAddress(addressElement: Element | null, context: string): Address {
    89→  if (!addressElement) {
    90→    throw new Error(`Missing address element in ${context}`)
    91→  }
    92→
    93→  return {
    94→    street: getTextContent(addressElement, 'street', `${context} address`),
    95→    city: getTextContent(addressElement, 'city', `${context} address`),
    96→    state: getTextContent(addressElement, 'state', `${context} address`),
    97→    zipCode: getTextContent(addressElement, 'zipCode', `${context} address`),
    98→  }
    99→}
   100→
   101→/**
   102→ * Validate XML for well-formedness and basic schema requirements
   103→ *
   104→ * @param xmlString - XML string to validate
   105→ * @returns ValidationResult with isValid flag and optional error message
   106→ */
   107→export function validateXml(xmlString: string): ValidationResult {
   108→  if (!xmlString || xmlString.trim() === '') {
   109→    return {
   110→      isValid: false,
   111→      error: 'XML input is empty. Please provide valid XML content.',
   112→    }
   113→  }
   114→
   115→  const parser = new DOMParser()
   116→  const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   117→
   118→  // Check for parser errors
   119→  const parserError = xmlDoc.querySelector('parsererror')
   120→  if (parserError) {
   121→    // Extract meaningful error message from parsererror element
   122→    const errorText = parserError.textContent || 'Unknown XML parsing error'
   123→
   124→    // Provide user-friendly error messages for common issues
   125→    if (errorText.includes('unclosed tag') || errorText.includes('Opening and ending tag mismatch')) {
   126→      return {
   127→        isValid: false,
   128→        error: 'XML has unclosed or mismatched tags. Please check that all opening tags have corresponding closing tags.',
   129→      }
   130→    }
   131→    if (errorText.includes('Unexpected end of file') || errorText.includes('premature end of data')) {
   132→      return {
   133→        isValid: false,
   134→        error: 'XML is incomplete. The document appears to end unexpectedly.',
   135→      }
   136→    }
   137→    if (errorText.includes('invalid character') || errorText.includes('not well-formed')) {
   138→      return {
   139→        isValid: false,
   140→        error: 'XML contains invalid characters or syntax. Please check for special characters that need to be escaped.',
   141→      }
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    return {
   145→      isValid: false,
   146→      error: `XML parsing error: ${errorText}`,
   147→    }
   148→  }
   149→
   150→  // Check for root element
   151→  const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   152→  if (!root || root.tagName !== 'applicationDocument') {
   153→    return {
   154→      isValid: false,
   155→      error: 'Invalid XML structure. Root element must be <applicationDocument>.',
   156→    }
   157→  }
   158→
   159→  // Check for required top-level elements
   160→  const requiredElements = ['applicant', 'date', 'recipient', 'letter']
   161→  for (const elementName of requiredElements) {
   162→    if (!root.querySelector(elementName)) {
   163→      return {
   164→        isValid: false,
   165→        error: `Missing required element: <${elementName}>. All application documents must include applicant, date, recipient, and letter sections.`,
   166→      }
   167→    }
   168→  }
   169→
   170→  return { isValid: true }
   171→}
   172→
   173→/**
   174→ * Parse XML string into structured data object
   175→ *
   176→ * @param xmlString - XML string to parse
   177→ * @returns ParseResult with success flag, parsed data, or error message
   178→ */
   179→export function parseXml(xmlString: string): ParseResult {
   180→  try {
   181→    // First validate the XML
   182→    const validation = validateXml(xmlString)
   183→    if (!validation.isValid) {
   184→      return {
   185→        success: false,
   186→        error: validation.error,
   187→      }
   188→    }
   189→
   190→    const parser = new DOMParser()
   191→    const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   192→    const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   193→
   194→    // Extract formatStyle attribute (optional)
   195→    const formatStyle = root.getAttribute('formatStyle') || undefined
   196→
   197→    // Parse applicant section
   198→    const applicantElement = root.querySelector('applicant')
   199→    if (!applicantElement) {
   200→      throw new Error('Missing required element: applicant')
   201→    }
   202→
   203→    const applicant: Applicant = {
   204→      name: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'name', 'applicant'),
   205→      address: parseAddress(applicantElement.querySelector('address'), 'applicant'),
   206→      contactInformation: {
   207→        phone: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation phone', 'applicant'),
   208→        email: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation email', 'applicant'),
   209→      },
   210→    }
   211→
   212→    // Parse date
   213→    const date = getTextContent(root, 'date')
   214→
   215→    // Parse recipient section
   216→    const recipientElement = root.querySelector('recipient')
   217→    if (!recipientElement) {
   218→      throw new Error('Missing required element: recipient')
   219→    }
   220→
   221→    const recipient: Recipient = {
   222→      position: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'position', 'recipient'),
   223→      company: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'company', 'recipient'),
   224→      address: parseAddress(recipientElement.querySelector('address'), 'recipient'),
   225→    }
   226→
   227→    // Parse letter section
   228→    const letterElement = root.querySelector('letter')
   229→    if (!letterElement) {
   230→      throw new Error('Missing required element: letter')
   231→    }
   232→
   233→    // Parse experiences
   234→    const experienceElements = letterElement.querySelectorAll('experienceSection experience')
   235→    const experiences: Experience[] = Array.from(experienceElements).map((expElement) => {
   236→      const employer = expElement.querySelector('employer')?.textContent?.trim() || ''
   237→      const achievementElements = expElement.querySelectorAll('achievements achievement')
   238→      const achievements: Achievement[] = Array.from(achievementElements).map(ach => ({
   239→        text: ach.textContent?.trim() || '',
   240→      }))
   241→
   242→      return {
   243→        employer,
   244→        achievements,
   245→      }
   246→    })
   247→
   248→    const letter: Letter = {
   249→      salutation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'salutation', 'letter'),
   250→      introduction: getTextContent(letterElement, 'introduction', 'letter'),
   251→      experienceSection: experiences,
   252→      motivation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'motivation', 'letter'),
   253→      closing: getTextContent(letterElement, 'closing', 'letter'),
   254→      signature: getTextContent(letterElement, 'signature', 'letter'),
   255→    }
   256→
   257→    const parsedData: ParsedData = {
   258→      formatStyle,
   259→      applicant,
   260→      date,
   261→      recipient,
   262→      letter,
   263→    }
   264→
   265→    return {
   266→      success: true,
   267→      data: parsedData,
   268→    }
   269→  }
   270→  catch (error) {
   271→    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred during parsing'
   272→    return {
   273→      success: false,
   274→      error: `Failed to parse XML: ${errorMessage}`,
   275→    }
   276→  }
   277→}
   278→
   279→/**
   280→ * Composable function to use XML parser in Vue components
   281→ */
   282→export function useXmlParser() {
   283→  return {
   284→    parseXml,
   285→    validateXml,
   286→  }
   287→}

USERMESSAGE #29
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Resignation Letter Parser Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides XML parsing and validation for resignation letter documents.
     5→ * Uses the same browser DOMParser approach as useXmlParser.ts.
     6→ *
     7→ * XML Schema:
     8→ * <resignationLetter>
     9→ *   <sender>
    10→ *     <name>...</name>
    11→ *     <position>...</position>
    12→ *   </sender>
    13→ *   <date>...</date>
    14→ *   <recipient>
    15→ *     <name>...</name>
    16→ *     <title>...</title>
    17→ *     <company>...</company>
    18→ *   </recipient>
    19→ *   <body>
    20→ *     <paragraph>...</paragraph>
    21→ *   </body>
    22→ *   <signature>
    23→ *     <name>...</name>
    24→ *     <position>...</position>
    25→ *   </signature>
    26→ * </resignationLetter>
    27→ */
    28→
    29→import type { ValidationResult, ParseResult } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'
    30→
    31→// ─── Type definitions ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    32→
    33→export interface ResignationSender {
    34→  name: string
    35→  position: string
    36→}
    37→
    38→export interface ResignationRecipient {
    39→  name: string
    40→  title: string
    41→  company: string
    42→}
    43→
    44→export interface ResignationSignature {
    45→  name: string
    46→  position: string
    47→}
    48→
    49→export interface ResignationParsedData {
    50→  sender: ResignationSender
    51→  date: string
    52→  recipient: ResignationRecipient
    53→  body: string[]
    54→  signature: ResignationSignature
    55→}
    56→
    57→// ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    58→
    59→function getText(parent: Element | null, selector: string): string {
    60→  if (!parent) return ''
    61→  return parent.querySelector(selector)?.textContent?.trim() ?? ''
    62→}
    63→
    64→// ─── Validate ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→export function validateResignationXml(xmlString: string): ValidationResult {
    67→  if (!xmlString || xmlString.trim() === '') {
    68→    return {
    69→      isValid: false,
    70→      error: 'XML input is empty. Please provide valid XML content.',
    71→    }
    72→  }
    73→
    74→  const parser = new DOMParser()
    75→  const doc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
    76→
    77→  const parserError = doc.querySelector('parsererror')
    78→  if (parserError) {
    79→    const errorText = parserError.textContent || 'Unknown XML parsing error'
    80→
    81→    if (errorText.includes('unclosed tag') || errorText.includes('Opening and ending tag mismatch')) {
    82→      return {
    83→        isValid: false,
    84→        error: 'XML has unclosed or mismatched tags. Please check that all opening tags have corresponding closing tags.',
    85→      }
    86→    }
    87→    if (errorText.includes('Unexpected end of file') || errorText.includes('premature end of data')) {
    88→      return {
    89→        isValid: false,
    90→        error: 'XML is incomplete. The document appears to end unexpectedly.',
    91→      }
    92→    }
    93→
    94→    return {
    95→      isValid: false,
    96→      error: `XML parsing error: ${errorText}`,
    97→    }
    98→  }
    99→
   100→  const root = doc.documentElement
   101→  if (!root || root.tagName !== 'resignationLetter') {
   102→    return {
   103→      isValid: false,
   104→      error: 'Invalid XML structure. Root element must be <resignationLetter>.',
   105→    }
   106→  }
   107→
   108→  const required = ['sender', 'date', 'recipient', 'body', 'signature']
   109→  for (const el of required) {
   110→    if (!root.querySelector(el)) {
   111→      return {
   112→        isValid: false,
   113→        error: `Missing required element: <${el}>. Resignation letters must include sender, date, recipient, body, and signature.`,
   114→      }
   115→    }
   116→  }
   117→
   118→  return { isValid: true }
   119→}
   120→
   121→// ─── Parse ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   122→
   123→export function parseResignationXml(xmlString: string): ParseResult {
   124→  try {
   125→    const validation = validateResignationXml(xmlString)
   126→    if (!validation.isValid) {
   127→      return { success: false, error: validation.error }
   128→    }
   129→
   130→    const parser = new DOMParser()
   131→    const doc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   132→    const root = doc.documentElement
   133→
   134→    const senderEl = root.querySelector('sender')
   135→    const recipientEl = root.querySelector('recipient')
   136→    const bodyEl = root.querySelector('body')
   137→    const signatureEl = root.querySelector('signature')
   138→
   139→    const sender: ResignationSender = {
   140→      name: getText(senderEl, 'name'),
   141→      position: getText(senderEl, 'position'),
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    const recipient: ResignationRecipient = {
   145→      name: getText(recipientEl, 'name'),
   146→      title: getText(recipientEl, 'title'),
   147→      company: getText(recipientEl, 'company'),
   148→    }
   149→
   150→    const body: string[] = bodyEl
   151→      ? Array.from(bodyEl.querySelectorAll('paragraph')).map(p => p.textContent?.trim() ?? '').filter(t => t)
   152→      : []
   153→
   154→    const signature: ResignationSignature = {
   155→      name: getText(signatureEl, 'name'),
   156→      position: getText(signatureEl, 'position'),
   157→    }
   158→
   159→    const data: ResignationParsedData = {
   160→      sender,
   161→      date: root.querySelector('date')?.textContent?.trim() ?? '',
   162→      recipient,
   163→      body,
   164→      signature,
   165→    }
   166→
   167→    return { success: true, data }
   168→  }
   169→  catch (error) {
   170→    const msg = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred during parsing'
   171→    return { success: false, error: `Failed to parse XML: ${msg}` }
   172→  }
   173→}
   174→

## Template System Exploration Report

I've completed a thorough exploration of the ohmydoc-v2 template system. Here's what I found:

### 1. **Template Directory Structure**

The application has 5 templates across 2 document types:

**Cover Letters (3 templates):**
- `/home/gem/project/templates/modern/` - Modern template
- `/home/gem/project/templates/classic/` - Classic template
- `/home/gem/project/templates/minimal/` - Minimal template

**Resignation Letters (2 templates):**
- `/home/gem/project/templates/resignation-professional/` - Professional resignation letter
- `/home/gem/project/templates/resignation-brief/` - Brief resignation letter

---

### 2. **useTemplate.ts - Template Management Composable**

**Location:** `/home/gem/project/composables/useTemplate.ts`

**Key Features:**
- **Template Registry:** Maps 5 templates to their Vue components and metadata
- **Metadata Interface:**
  ```typescript
  interface TemplateMetadata {
    name: string
    displayName: string
    description: string
    documentTypes: string[]  // e.g., ['cover-letter'] or ['resignation-letter']
  }
  ```

- **Core Functions:**
  - `useTemplate()` - Composable for reactive template selection
  - `setActiveTemplate(name: string)` - Switch templates and persist to localStorage
  - `currentTemplate` - Computed reactive component
  - `currentTemplateMetadata` - Computed metadata
  - `getAvailableTemplates()` - All registered template names
  - `getAllTemplateMetadata()` - All metadata objects
  - `getTemplatesForDocumentType(docType: string)` - Filter templates by document type

- **State Management:**
  - Uses `useState()` for shared reactive state across components
  - Persists to `localStorage` with key `'ohmydoc_template'`
  - Restores on component mount

---

### 3. **useXmlParser.ts - Cover Letter Parser**

**Location:** `/home/gem/project/composables/useXmlParser.ts`

**ParsedData Type (for cover letters):**
```typescript
export interface ParsedData {
  formatStyle?: string
  applicant: Applicant
  date: string
  recipient: Recipient
  letter: Letter
}

interface Applicant {
  name: string
  address: Address
  contactInformation: ContactInformation
}

interface Address {
  street: string
  city: string
  state: string
  zipCode: string
}

interface ContactInformation {
  phone: string
  email: string
}

interface Recipient {
  position: string
  company: string
  address: Address
}

interface Letter {
  salutation: string
  introduction: string
  experienceSection: Experience[]
  motivation: string
  closing: string
  signature: string
}

interface Experience {
  employer: string
  achievements: Achievement[]
}

interface Achievement {
  text: string
}
```

**Key Functions:**
- `parseXml(xmlString)` - Parse XML into ParsedData
- `validateXml(xmlString)` - Validate before parsing (checks well-formedness, required elements)
- Uses browser's native `DOMParser` API (zero dependencies)

---

### 4. **useResignationParser.ts - Resignation Letter Parser**

**Location:** `/home/gem/project/composables/useResignationParser.ts`

**ResignationParsedData Type:**
```typescript
export interface ResignationParsedData {
  sender: ResignationSender
  date: string
  recipient: ResignationRecipient
  body: string[]
  signature: ResignationSignature
}

interface ResignationSender {
  name: string
  position: string
}

interface ResignationRecipient {
  name: string
  title: string
  company: string
}

interface ResignationSignature {
  name: string
  position: string
}
```

**Key Functions:**
- `parseResignationXml(xmlString)` - Parse resignation XML
- `validateResignationXml(xmlString)` - Validate resignation structure

---

### 5. **Cover Letter Templates Structure**

All three cover letter templates follow this pattern:

**Props Interface (identical across all templates):**
```typescript
interface Props {
  data: ParsedData
}
```

#### **a) Modern Template** (`CoverLetterModern.vue`)
- **Structure:** Semantic HTML using `<article>`, `<header>`, `<main>`
- **Styling Approach:** CSS imported as module in `<script setup>` to ensure reliable bundling
- **CSS Features:**
  - Design system variables: `--ink: #111`, `--muted: #555`, `--accent: #0f6fec`
  - Typography: serif body (`--font-body`), sans-serif UI (`--font-ui`)
  - Responsive design with `clamp()` for fluid typography
  - Print optimization with `@media print`
  - Mobile responsive with `@media screen and (max-width: 768px)`

#### **b) Classic Template** (`CoverLetterClassic.vue`)
- **Structure:** Table-based layout (traditional format)
- **Design Choices:**
  - Header table with bottom border
  - Recipient section with left accent border (3px, --accent color)
  - Uppercase applicant name with letter-spacing
  - Square bullets for achievements (vs. disc in modern)
  - Formal, traditional styling

#### **c) Minimal Template** (`CoverLetterMinimal.vue`)
- **Structure:** Plain divs with generous whitespace
- **Design Choices:**
  - Lighter font-weight on name (400 vs 600)
  - Larger line-height (1.7 vs 1.6) for readability
  - Custom bullet style: em-dash (—) rendered via `::before` pseudo-element
  - Minimal styling, maximum whitespace
  - Extra padding (3rem) for spacious feel

---

### 6. **Resignation Letter Templates Structure**

Both resignation templates use different props type: `ResignationParsedData`

**Props Interface:**
```typescript
interface Props {
  data: ResignationParsedData
}
```

#### **a) Professional Template** (`ResignationProfessional.vue`)
- **Structure:** `<article>` with formal letterhead layout
- **Layout:**
  - Header: sender info (left) + date (right) using flexbox `justify-content: space-between`
  - Horizontal divider (`<hr>` with styled border)
  - Recipient block
  - Body paragraphs (array of strings)
  - Signature block
- **Styling:**
  - Max-width: 720px
  - Text justification (`text-align: justify`) on paragraphs
  - Responsive: header stacks on mobile (`flex-direction: column-reverse`)

#### **b) Brief Template** (`ResignationBrief.vue`)
- **Structure:** Compact divs, all essentials on minimal lines
- **Layout:**
  - Single-line header: name · position (date pushed right with `margin-left: auto`)
  - Single-line recipient: name · title · company
  - Body paragraphs
  - Minimal signature line
- **Styling:**
  - Max-width: 640px (narrower than professional)
  - Smaller font-sizes overall (0.85rem header, 0.82rem recipient)
  - Border-bottom on recipient section
  - Minimal spacing (1.75rem margins)

---

### 7. **CSS Architecture Pattern**

All templates follow this consistent pattern:

**File Structure:**
```
templates/{name}/
├── CoverLetter{Name}.vue    (or Resignation{Name}.vue)
└── styles.css
```

**CSS Import Strategy (from CLAUDE.md):**
```vue
<script setup>
import './styles.css'  // Import as module in script
// This ensures reliable loading across all platforms (including Vercel)
</script>

<style scoped>
/* Empty scoped block applies Vue's data-v-* scoping */
</style>
```

**Why this approach:**
- Avoids `@import './styles.css'` in `<style scoped>` block (had Vercel issues)
- Avoids `<style scoped src="./styles.css">` (also had issues)
- Script import ensures CSS is bundled correctly
- Empty scoped block applies Vue's scoping mechanism

---

### 8. **Design System (Shared Across All Templates)**

**Color Palette:**
- `--ink: #111` (primary text color)
- `--muted: #555` (secondary text, metadata)
- `--accent: #0f6fec` (links, highlights)

**Typography:**
- `--font-body: ui-serif, Georgia, "Times New Roman", Times, serif`
- `--font-ui: ui-sans-serif, system-ui, -apple-system, Segoe UI, Roboto, Helvetica, Arial, ...`

**Spacing & Sizing:**
- Cover letters: `--max-width: 720px` (modern), `680px` (minimal)
- Resignation letters: `--max-width: 720px` (professional), `640px` (brief)
- Standard line-height: 1.6-1.7
- Gap units: `--gap: 0.9rem`, `--gap-lg: 1.25rem`

**Responsive:**
- Mobile breakpoint: `@media screen and (max-width: 768px)`
- Resignation brief: additional breakpoint at `600px`

**Print Optimization:**
- Removes padding and margins
- Sets `margin: 0 2cm` for print spacing
- Removes link styling for printed output

---

| Aspect | Modern | Classic | Minimal | Resignation Pro | Resignation Brief |
|--------|--------|---------|---------|-----------------|-------------------|

| **Achievements List** | Disc bullets | Square bullets | Em-dash (custom) | N/A | N/A |
| **Recipient Border** | None | Left border (accent) | None | Horizontal rule | Bottom border |
| **Name Weight** | 600 | 700 | 400 (lighter) | 600 | 600 |
| **Line Height** | 1.6 | 1.6 | 1.7 (spacious) | 1.65 | 1.6 |
| **Max Width** | 720px | 720px | 680px | 720px | 640px |
| **Data Type** | `ParsedData` | `ParsedData` | `ParsedData` | `ResignationParsedData` | `ResignationParsedData` |

### 10. **Document Type Support**

The system supports filtering templates by document type via `documentTypes` array in metadata:

**Cover Letter Templates:**
- modern → `documentTypes: ['cover-letter']`
- classic → `documentTypes: ['cover-letter']`
- minimal → `documentTypes: ['cover-letter']`

**Resignation Letter Templates:**
- resignation-professional → `documentTypes: ['resignation-letter']`
- resignation-brief → `documentTypes: ['resignation-letter']`

Use `getTemplatesForDocumentType('resignation-letter')` to get only resignation templates.

    18→
    19→// Template metadata interface
    20→export interface TemplateMetadata {
    21→  name: string
    22→  displayName: string
    23→  description: string
    24→  /** Document type names this template supports (matches DocumentTypeConfig.name) */
    25→  documentTypes: string[]
    26→}

    28→// Template registry type

    30→  [key: string]: {
    31→    component: Component
    32→    metadata: TemplateMetadata
    33→  }
    34→}
    35→

    37→ * Template Registry

    89→
    90→/**
    91→ * Composable function to use the reactive template system in Vue components.
    92→ *
    93→ * Active template state is shared across all component instances via useState.
    94→ * On mount, the saved localStorage value is restored (client-side only).
    95→ *
    96→ * @returns Reactive template state and control functions
    97→ */
    98→export function useTemplate() {
    99→  // Shared reactive state — useState ensures all components see the same value
   100→  const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => 'modern')
   101→
   102→  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only, runs once per component mount)
   103→  onMounted(() => {
   104→    try {
   105→      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
   106→      if (saved && templates[saved]) {
   107→        activeTemplate.value = saved
   108→      }
   109→    }
   110→    catch {
   111→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
   112→    }
   113→  })
   114→
   115→  /**
   116→   * Switch to a different template and persist the choice to localStorage.
   117→   */
   118→  function setActiveTemplate(name: string) {
   119→    if (!templates[name]) {
   120→      console.warn(`Template "${name}" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`)
   121→      return
   122→    }
   123→    activeTemplate.value = name
   124→    try {
   125→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)
   126→    }
   127→    catch {
   128→      // Ignore storage errors
   129→    }
   130→  }
   131→
   132→  /** Reactive component for the currently active template */
   133→  const currentTemplate = computed<Component | undefined>(
   134→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.component,
   135→  )
   136→
   137→  /** Metadata for the currently active template */
   138→  const currentTemplateMetadata = computed<TemplateMetadata | undefined>(
   139→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.metadata,
   140→  )
   141→
   142→  /** Names of all registered templates */
   143→  function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   144→    return Object.keys(templates)
   145→  }
   146→
   147→  /** Metadata objects for all registered templates */
   148→  function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   149→    return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   150→  }
   151→
   152→  /** Metadata objects for templates that support the given document type */
   153→  function getTemplatesForDocumentType(docType: string): TemplateMetadata[] {
   154→    return Object.values(templates)
   155→      .filter(t => t.metadata.documentTypes.includes(docType))
   156→      .map(t => t.metadata)
   157→  }
   158→
   159→  return {
   160→    activeTemplate,
   161→    setActiveTemplate,
   162→    currentTemplate,
   163→    currentTemplateMetadata,
   164→    getAvailableTemplates,
   165→    getAllTemplateMetadata,
   166→    getTemplatesForDocumentType,
   167→  }
   168→}

## Status DONE ## What Changed - `templates/executive/CoverLetterExecutive.vue` — new template: semantic HTML with large uppercase name, two horizontal rule dividers, serif body - `templates/executive/styles.css` — navy accent (`#1a3a5c`), Georgia serif, uppercase letter-spaced name at 2.4rem, square list bullets, italic employer names - `templates/creative/CoverLetterCreative.vue` — new template: two-column grid layout with sidebar `<aside>` + `<main>` content area - `templates/creative/styles.css` — purple sidebar (`#5e60ce`) with white text, sans-serif throughout, circular accent bullets (`#48bfe3`), collapses to single column on ≤640px; `print-color-adjust: exact` so sidebar background prints - `composables/useTemplate.ts` — imported and registered both new templates with `documentTypes: ['cover-letter']` ## Key Decisions - **Creative uses a two-column CSS grid** (sidebar + main) rather than a flat structure — breaks from other templates but gives the strongest visual differentiation for a creative audience - **`print-color-adjust: exact`** added to the Creative sidebar so the background color actually prints; the other templates don't need this since they're white-background - Resignation templates already existed (`resignation-professional`, `resignation-brief`), no changes made there ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feat/new-templates` - PR: https://github.com/kimwwk/ohmydoc-using-claude-code-agent/pull/27
